   function loadJSSuccessCallback (bundle) {
      if ( typeof( loadJSSuccessCallbacks[bundle] ) !== 'function' ) return;
      loadJSSuccessCallbacks[bundle]();
    }
    function fireLoadJSBundle (bundle) {
      if ( typeof( loadJSBundles[bundle] ) !== 'function' ) return;
      loadJSBundles[bundle]();
    }

    var loadJSSuccessCallbacks = {
      social: function () {
        $('.sticky-panel-container > .sticky-panel').show();
        return true;
      },
    };
    var loadJSBundles = {
      'adsense': function () {
        if ( loadjs.isDefined( 'adsense' ) ) return false;
        loadjs( ["https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js"], 'adsense', {
          success: function() {
            loadJSSuccessCallback( 'adsense' );
          },
          numRetries: 3,
        });
      },
      'gpt': function () {
        if ( loadjs.isDefined( 'gpt' ) ) return false;
        loadjs( ["https://www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js"], 'gpt', {
          success: function() {
            loadJSSuccessCallback( 'gpt' );
          },
          numRetries: 3,
        });
      },
      'social': function () {
        if ( loadjs.isDefined( 'social' ) ) return false;
        loadjs( ["https://cdn01.allafrica.com/static/js/facebook.min.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn08.allafrica.com/static/js/twitter.min.js?v=2021030600"], 'social', {
          success: function() {
            loadJSSuccessCallback( 'social' );
          },
          numRetries: 3,
        });
      },
      'tracking': function () {
        if ( loadjs.isDefined( 'tracking' ) ) return false;
        loadjs( ["https://cdn03.allafrica.com/static/js/quantcast.min.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn01.allafrica.com/static/js/alexa.min.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn09.allafrica.com/static/js/comscore.min.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn03.allafrica.com/static/js/cxense.min.js?v=2021030600","https://www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js"], 'tracking', {
          success: function() {
            loadJSSuccessCallback( 'tracking' );
          },
          numRetries: 3,
        });
      },
    };

        <script>
         _ready.push(function($) {
    function toLocaleDateStringSupportsLocales() {
      try {
        new Date().toLocaleTimeString('i');
      } catch (e) {
        return e.name === 'RangeError';
      }
      return false;
    }
if ( ! loadjs.isDefined( 'mapael-maps-assets' ) ) {
  loadjs( ["https://cdn09.allafrica.com/static/js/jquery/jquery.mousewheel-3.1.13.min.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn04.allafrica.com/static/js/mapael/raphael-2.2.0.min.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn07.allafrica.com/static/js/mapael/jquery.mapael-2.2.0.js?v=2021030600","https://cdn06.allafrica.com/static/js/mapael/africa_countries.js?v=2021030600"], 'mapael-maps-assets', {
    async: false,
    numRetries: 3,
  });
}

    loadjs.ready('mapael-maps-assets', {
      success: function() {
        $(function () {

          // Get the data
          var areas = {},
            totals = {
             cases     : 0,
             recoveries: 0,
             deaths    : 0
            };
            var labels = {"covid_map_total_deaths":"Total Deaths","covid_map_total_cases":"Total Cases","last_updated":"Last Updated","continent_wide":"Continent-wide","covid_map_mouseover_hint":"Hover over any country to see detailed data","covid_map_total_recoveries":"Total Recoveries"};
          $.getJSON("/functions/covid19-data.json", function (data) {
            var lastUpdated;
            var canFormatDate = toLocaleDateStringSupportsLocales;
            $.each(data, function (id, elem) {
              var area = {};
              area.value = '' +elem.TotalConfirmed;
              area.href = "#covid19-map";
              area.tooltip = {
                content:
                  "<span style='font-weight:bold;'>" + elem.Country + "</span>" + "<br/>" +
                  labels.covid_map_total_cases + " : " + elem.TotalConfirmed + "<br/>" +
                  labels.covid_map_total_recoveries + " : " + elem.TotalRecovered + "<br/>" +
                  labels.covid_map_total_deaths + " : " + elem.TotalDeaths
              };
              areas[id] = area;
              totals.cases += parseInt(elem.TotalConfirmed);
              totals.recoveries += parseInt(elem.TotalRecovered);
              totals.deaths += parseInt(elem.TotalDeaths);
              if ( canFormatDate && elem.Date && lastUpdated===undefined ) {
                try {
                  var date = new Date();
                  date.setTime( Date.parse( elem.Date ) );
                  var options = { hour12: false, year: 'numeric', month: 'short', day: 'numeric', timeZone: 'UTC', timeZoneName: 'short' };
                  lastUpdated = date.toLocaleTimeString( 'en-US', options);
                } catch (e) {
                  lastUpdated = '';
                }
              }
            });

            $("#covid19-map").show();
            function numberWithCommas(x) {
              return x.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ",");
            }
            if( totals.cases ) {
              $("#summary-info").append('<table><tr><td colspan="2">'+labels.continent_wide+'</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>'+labels.covid_map_total_cases+'</td><td>'+numberWithCommas(totals.cases)+'</td></tr><tr><td>'+labels.covid_map_total_recoveries+'</td><td>'+numberWithCommas(totals.recoveries)+'</td></tr><tr><td>'+labels.covid_map_total_deaths+'</td><td>'+numberWithCommas(totals.deaths)+'</td></tr></table>');
            }
            if( lastUpdated ) {
              $("#covid19-map-last-updated").append(labels.last_updated + ': ' + lastUpdated);
            }
            $(".mapcontainer").mapael({
              map: {
                name: "africa_countries",
                defaultArea: {
                  attrs: {
                    "fill": "#eee",
                    "stroke": "#333",
                    "stroke-miterlimit": "4",
                    "stroke-width": ".75",
                  },
                  attrsHover: {
                    "fill": "#9ce76f",
                  }
                }
              },
              legend: {
                area: {
                  mode: "vertical",
                  title: "Covid-19 Cases in Africa",
                  titleAttrs: {
                      fill: "#666",
                      "stroke": "#666",
                  },
                  labelAttrs: {
                    fill: "#666",
                    "stroke": "#666",
                  },
                  labelAttrsHover: {
                      fill: "#666",
                  },
                  slices: [
                    {
                      max: 0,
                      attrs: {
                        fill: "#eee"
                      },
                      label: "No data"
                    },
                    {
                      min: 0,
                      max: 2000,
                      attrs: {
                        fill: "#f0f000"
                      },
                      label: "Less than 2000"
                    },
                    {
                      min: 2000,
                      max: 10000,
                      attrs: {
                        fill: "#f0aa00"
                      },
                      label: "Between 2000 and 10000"
                    },
                    {
                      min: 10000,
                      max: 30000,
                      attrs: {
                        fill: "#f04f00"
                      },
                      label: "Between 10000 and 30000"
                    },
                    {
                      min: 30000,
                      max: 250000,
                      attrs: {
                        fill: "#f00000"
                      },
                      label: "Between 30000 and 250000"
                    },
                    {
                      min: 250000,
                      attrs: {
                        fill: "#c80000"
                      },
                      label: "Greater than 250000"
                    }
                  ]
                },
              },
              areas: areas,
            });
            $(".mapcontainer > .map").append('<div class="mouseover-hint">' + labels.covid_map_mouseover_hint + '</div>');
          });
        });
      }
    });
  });
        </script>

  <script>
   function loadAds () {
    var args = Object.assign(
          {
            requestNonPersonalizedAds: 1,
          },
          arguments[0]
        ),
        requestNonPersonalizedAds = args.requestNonPersonalizedAds,
        m2hbEnabled = false;
    if ( isOperaMini ) m2hbEnabled = false;
    try {
      fireLoadJSBundle( 'gpt' );
      fireDFP({
        m2hbEnabled: m2hbEnabled,
        requestNonPersonalizedAds: requestNonPersonalizedAds,
      });
    } catch(e) { logError(e); }
    try {
      fireLoadJSBundle( 'adsense' );
      configureAdSense({
        googleAdClient: "ca-pub-2420009840005975",
        enablePageLevelAds: true,
        requestNonPersonalizedAds: requestNonPersonalizedAds,
      });
    } catch(e) { logError(e); }
  }
  function loadTracking () {
    fireLoadJSBundle( 'tracking' );
    initEventTools($)
  }
  function loadSocial () {
    fireLoadJSBundle( 'social' );
    if ( 'loadA2A' in window ) window.loadA2A();
  }
  </script>
  <script>
   function triggerConsentAction () {
    var args = Object.assign(
      {
        consentState: undefined,
      },
      arguments[0]
    );

    if ( typeof( args.consentState ) === 'undefined' ) {
      _ready.push(function($) {
        loadConsented();
      });
    } else if ( args.consentState === null ) {
      // non-EEA user
      _ready.push(function($) {
        loadConsented();
        $('.change-privacy-settings').remove();
      });
    } else {
      // EEA user
      _ready.push(function($) {
        if ( ! Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call( window, '__tcfapi' ) ) return loadNonConsented();
        window.__tcfapi('getTCData', null, function (consentData, consentDataSuccess) {
          window.__tcfapi( 'getPublisherConsents', null, function( publisherConsents, publisherConsentsSuccess ) {
          });
          window.__tcfapi( 'getVendorConsents', null, function( vendorConsents, vendorConsentsSuccess ) {
            if ( ! vendorConsentsSuccess ) return loadNonConsented();
            if ( ! vendorConsents.gdprApplies ) return loadConsented();
            if ( vendorConsents.purposeConsents && vendorConsents.purposeConsents[1] && vendorConsents.purposeConsents[3] )
              return loadConsented();
            return loadNonConsented();
          });
        });

      });

    } // end EEA-user
  }

  (function () {
    if ( clickioConsentCallback.fired && clickioConsentCallback.consentState !== 'UNSET' ) {
      return triggerConsentAction({
        consentState: clickioConsentCallback.consentState,
      });
    } // end if fired

    (window.__lxG__consent__= window.__lxG__consent__||{}).consentCallback = function( consentState ) {
      // EEA user, consent interface shown, cmp loaded, user has not decided yet
      if ( consentState === -1 ) return;

      clickioConsentCallback.fired = true;
      clickioConsentCallback.consentState = consentState;

      return triggerConsentAction({
        consentState: consentState,
      });
    }; // close consentCallback
  })();
  </script>
